##############################################################################################
###   Cosmetic Nation articles & flexions / Articles et flexions pour les pays maquillés   ###
##############################################################################################
#Ex.: LE Royaume de Libye / DU Royaume de Libye / DU Royaume de Libye / AU Royaume de Libye / DANS LE Royaume de Libye
frloc_cosmtags_sg_masc_cons_dansle_01 = {
	OR = {
		AND = { has_cosmetic_tag = jimma has_government = fascism NOT = { is_subject_of = ITA } } # jimma_fascism
		AND = { has_cosmetic_tag = jimma has_government = neutrality } # jimma_neutrality
		AND = { has_cosmetic_tag = gojjam OR = { has_government = neutrality has_government = democratic AND = { is_subject_of = ITA has_government = fascism } } } # gojjam OR gojjam_neutrality OR gojjam_democratic OR gojjam_ITA_fascism_subject
		AND = { OR = { tag = RAJ original_tag = RAJ } has_cosmetic_tag = RAJ_UK OR = { has_government = democratic has_government = neutrality } } # RAJ_UK_democratic OR RAJ_UK_neutrality
		AND = { OR = { tag = RAJ original_tag = RAJ } has_cosmetic_tag = RAJ_UK is_subject = yes } # RAJ_UK_subject
		AND = { OR = { tag = RAJ original_tag = RAJ } has_cosmetic_tag = RAJ_UK has_autonomy_state = autonomy_dominion } # RAJ_UK_autonomy_dominion
		AND = { OR = { tag = CAN original_tag = CAN } has_cosmetic_tag = CAN_UK has_autonomy_state = autonomy_dominion } # CAN_UK_autonomy_dominion
		AND = { OR = { tag = USA original_tag = USA } has_cosmetic_tag = USA_UK has_autonomy_state = autonomy_dominion } # USA_UK_autonomy_dominion
		AND = { OR = { tag = USA original_tag = USA } has_cosmetic_tag = USA_SAF_EDW has_autonomy_state = autonomy_dominion } # USA_SAF_EDW_autonomy_dominion
		AND = { OR = { tag = LBA original_tag = LBA } is_subject_of = GER has_autonomy_state = autonomy_colony } # LBA_GER_autonomy_colony
		AND = { OR = { tag = LBA original_tag = LBA } is_subject_of = GER has_autonomy_state = autonomy_reichsprotectorate } # LBA_GER_autonomy_reichsprotectorate
		AND = { OR = { tag = LBA original_tag = LBA } is_subject_of = GER has_autonomy_state = autonomy_puppet has_government = fascism } # LBA_GER_fascism_autonomy_puppet
		AND = { OR = { tag = LBA original_tag = LBA } is_subject_of = ITA has_government = fascism OR = { has_autonomy_state = autonomy_satellite has_autonomy_state = autonomy_dominion } } # LBA_ITA_fascism_autonomy_satellite OR LBA_ITA_fascism_autonomy_dominion
		AND = { OR = { tag = KEN original_tag = KEN } is_subject_of = GER has_autonomy_state = autonomy_colony } # KEN_GER_autonomy_colony
		AND = { OR = { tag = KEN original_tag = KEN } is_subject_of = GER has_autonomy_state = autonomy_reichsprotectorate } # KEN_GER_autonomy_reichsprotectorate
		AND = { OR = { tag = KEN original_tag = KEN } is_subject_of = GER has_autonomy_state = autonomy_puppet has_government = fascism } # KEN_GER_fascism_autonomy_puppet
		AND = { OR = { tag = ZIM original_tag = ZIM } is_subject_of = GER has_autonomy_state = autonomy_colony } # ZIM_GER_autonomy_colony
		AND = { OR = { tag = ZIM original_tag = ZIM } is_subject_of = GER has_autonomy_state = autonomy_reichsprotectorate } # ZIM_GER_autonomy_reichsprotectorate
		AND = { OR = { tag = ZIM original_tag = ZIM } is_subject_of = GER has_autonomy_state = autonomy_puppet has_government = fascism } # ZIM_GER_fascism_autonomy_puppet
		AND = { OR = { tag = KEN original_tag = KEN } is_subject_of = ENG has_autonomy_state = autonomy_dominion } # KEN_ENG_autonomy_dominion
